if (!is_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') != '8dfcc50a5b1c6967c74466128ba836a8e4b43106') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '8dfcc50a5b1c6967c74466128ba836a8e4b43106') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '4fc27917d29719c66123fde8577e3d89ab552d80') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '8dfcc50a5b1c6967c74466128ba836a8e4b43106') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.css');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.css') != 'b88509b9b04f740cb9c31a99a8dd4ea533c80202') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== 'b88509b9b04f740cb9c31a99a8dd4ea533c80202') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '6dfed804573efb4b3bf6adbc42fec1dc92ca1978') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== 'b88509b9b04f740cb9c31a99a8dd4ea533c80202') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.js');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.js') != 'b73d0934d3d094039ca8899e4d620762f6c25b7b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== 'b73d0934d3d094039ca8899e4d620762f6c25b7b') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '25bd5ed5805134acfdc2d984c9036a9ba911060a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== 'b73d0934d3d094039ca8899e4d620762f6c25b7b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 9\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 9') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
